</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The input string to search. String.</li><li><code>pattern</code>: The regular expression pattern to match, using re2 regular expression syntax. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The first substring that matches the <code>pattern</code>. If the <code>pattern</code> contains capturing groups, it returns the match for the first capturing group. Returns an empty string if no match is found. String.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT extract(&#x27;number: 1, number: 2, number: 3&#x27;, &#x27;\\d+&#x27;) AS result
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─result─┐
│ 1      │
└────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="extractall" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">extractAll<a class="headerlink" href="#extractall" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Extracts all substrings from <code>haystack</code> that match the provided regular expression <code>pattern</code>.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">extractAll(haystack, pattern)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The input string to search. String.</li><li><code>pattern</code>: The regular expression pattern to match, using re2 regular expression syntax. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>An array of all substrings that match the <code>pattern</code>. If the <code>pattern</code> contains capturing groups, it returns matches for the first capturing group. Returns an empty array if no matches are found. Array(String).</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT extractAll(&#x27;number: 1, number: 2, number: 3&#x27;, &#x27;\\d+&#x27;) AS result
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─result────────┐
│ [&#x27;1&#x27;,&#x27;2&#x27;,&#x27;3&#x27;] │
└───────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="extractallgroupshorizontal" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">extractAllGroupsHorizontal<a class="headerlink" href="#extractallgroupshorizontal" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Extracts all matches for each capturing group in a regular expression, returning an array of arrays where each inner array contains all matches for a specific group.</p><p>This function is slower than <code>extractAllGroupsVertical</code>.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">extractAllGroupsHorizontal(haystack, pattern)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The input string to search. String.</li><li><code>pattern</code>: The regular expression pattern with capturing groups, using re2 regular expression syntax. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>An array of arrays of strings. The first inner array contains all matches for the first capturing group, the second for the second, and so on. Array(Array(String)).</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>If <code>haystack</code> doesn&#x27;t match the <code>pattern</code> regex, an array of empty arrays is returned.</p></div></div><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT extractAllGroupsHorizontal(&#x27;abc=111, def=222, ghi=333&#x27;, &#x27;(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)=(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)&#x27;)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─extractAllGroupsHorizontal(&#x27;abc=111, def=222, ghi=333&#x27;, &#x27;(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)=(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)&#x27;)─┐
│ [[&#x27;abc&#x27;,&#x27;def&#x27;,&#x27;ghi&#x27;],[&#x27;111&#x27;,&#x27;222&#x27;,&#x27;333&#x27;]]                                                │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="extractgroups" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">extractGroups<a class="headerlink" href="#extractgroups" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Extracts the first set of matches for all capturing groups in a regular expression.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">extractGroups(haystack, pattern)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The input string to search. String.</li><li><code>pattern</code>: The regular expression pattern with capturing groups, using re2 regular expression syntax. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>An array of strings, where each element corresponds to the first match of a capturing group. Array(String).</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT extractGroups(&#x27;hello abc=111 world&#x27;, &#x27;(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)=(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)&#x27;) AS result
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─result────────┐
│ [&#x27;abc&#x27;,&#x27;111&#x27;] │
└───────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="extractallgroupsvertical" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">extractAllGroupsVertical<a class="headerlink" href="#extractallgroupsvertical" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Extracts all matches for all capturing groups in a regular expression, returning an array of arrays where each inner array represents a complete match of all groups.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">extractAllGroupsVertical(haystack, pattern)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The input string to search. String.</li><li><code>pattern</code>: The regular expression pattern with capturing groups, using re2 regular expression syntax. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>An array of arrays of strings. Each inner array contains the matches for all capturing groups from a single overall match of the pattern. Array(Array(String)).</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>If <code>haystack</code> doesn&#x27;t match the <code>pattern</code> regex, an empty array is returned.</p></div></div><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT extractAllGroupsVertical(&#x27;abc=111, def=222, ghi=333&#x27;, &#x27;(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)=(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)&#x27;)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─extractAllGroupsVertical(&#x27;abc=111, def=222, ghi=333&#x27;, &#x27;(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)=(&quot;[^&quot;]+&quot;|\\w+)&#x27;)─┐

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Alias: <code>haystack LIKE pattern</code> (operator)</p><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The string to search within. String.</li><li><code>pattern</code>: The <code>LIKE</code> pattern to match. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Returns 1 if the <code>haystack</code> matches the <code>pattern</code>, otherwise returns 0. UInt8.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT like(&#x27;Tinybird&#x27;, &#x27;Tiny%bird&#x27;)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─like(&#x27;Tinybird&#x27;, &#x27;Tiny%bird&#x27;)─┐
│                             1 │
└───────────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="notlike" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">notLike<a class="headerlink" href="#notlike" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Checks if a string does NOT match a pattern using SQL <code>LIKE</code> syntax. This is the inverse of the <code>like</code> function.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">notLike(haystack, pattern)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Alias: <code>haystack NOT LIKE pattern</code> (operator)</p><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The string to search within. String.</li><li><code>pattern</code>: The <code>LIKE</code> pattern to match. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Returns 1 if the <code>haystack</code> does not match the <code>pattern</code>, otherwise returns 0. UInt8.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT notLike(&#x27;Tinybird&#x27;, &#x27;Tiny%house&#x27;)

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Alias: <code>haystack ILIKE pattern</code> (operator)</p><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The string to search within. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Returns 1 if the <code>haystack</code> matches the <code>pattern</code> (case-insensitive), otherwise returns 0. UInt8.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT ilike(&#x27;Tinybird&#x27;, &#x27;tiny%bird&#x27;)

This is the inverse of the <code>ilike</code> function.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">notILike(haystack, pattern)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Alias: <code>haystack NOT ILIKE pattern</code> (operator)</p><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The string to search within. String.</li><li><code>pattern</code>: The <code>LIKE</code> pattern to match. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Returns 1 if the <code>haystack</code> does not match the <code>pattern</code> (case-insensitive), otherwise returns 0. UInt8.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT notILike(&#x27;Tinybird&#x27;, &#x27;tiny%house&#x27;)

└────────────────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="ngramdistance" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">ngramDistance<a class="headerlink" href="#ngramdistance" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Calculates the 4-gram distance between two strings, indicating their similarity. A value closer to 0 means higher similarity, while a value closer to 1 means lower similarity.</p><p>Functions <code>ngramDistanceCaseInsensitive</code>, <code>ngramDistanceUTF8</code>, <code>ngramDistanceCaseInsensitiveUTF8</code> provide case-insensitive and/or UTF-8 variants of this function.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">ngramDistance(haystack, needle)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The first string for comparison. String.</li><li><code>needle</code>: The second string for comparison. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>A Float32 value between 0 and 1, representing the normalized 4-gram distance. Float32.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The more similar two strings are to each other, the closer the result will be to 0 (identical).</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT ngramDistance(&#x27;Tinybird&#x27;,&#x27;Tinybird!&#x27;)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">0.06666667

String.</li><li><code>needle</code>: The second string for comparison. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>A Float32 value between 0 and 1, representing the normalized 4-gram distance, ignoring case. Float32.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>With <code>ngramDistance</code> differences in case will affect the similarity value:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT ngramDistance(&#x27;Tinybird&#x27;,&#x27;tinybird&#x27;)

A higher value (closer to 1) suggests a higher likelihood of <code>needle</code> being contained within <code>haystack</code>.</p><p>Functions <code>ngramSearchCaseInsensitive</code>, <code>ngramSearchUTF8</code>, <code>ngramSearchCaseInsensitiveUTF8</code> provide case-insensitive and/or UTF-8 variants of this function.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">ngramSearch(haystack, needle)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The string to search within. String.</li><li><code>needle</code>: The string to search for. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>A Float32 value between 0 and 1, representing the likelihood of <code>needle</code> being in <code>haystack</code>. Float32.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT ngramSearch(&#x27;Hello World&#x27;,&#x27;World Hello&#x27;)

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: String in which the search is performed. String or Enum.</li><li><code>needle</code>: Substring to be counted. String.</li><li><code>start_pos</code>: Position (1-based) in <code>haystack</code> at which the search starts. UInt. Optional.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The total number of times the <code>needle</code> substring appears in the <code>haystack</code>. UInt64.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT countSubstrings(&#x27;aaaa&#x27;, &#x27;aa&#x27;)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─countSubstrings(&#x27;aaaa&#x27;, &#x27;aa&#x27;)─┐

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: String in which the search is performed. String or Enum.</li><li><code>needle</code>: Substring to be counted. String.</li><li><code>start_pos</code>: Position (1-based) in <code>haystack</code> at which the search starts. UInt. Optional.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The total number of times the <code>needle</code> substring appears in the <code>haystack</code>, ignoring case. UInt64.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT countSubstringsCaseInsensitive(&#x27;AAAA&#x27;, &#x27;aa&#x27;)

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: UTF-8 encoded string in which the search is performed. UInt64.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT countSubstringsCaseInsensitiveUTF8(&#x27;ложка, кошка, картошка&#x27;, &#x27;КА&#x27;)

└──────────────────────────────────────────────┘
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="regexpextract" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">regexpExtract<a class="headerlink" href="#regexpextract" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Extracts a specific capturing group from the first match of a regular expression in a string.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">regexpExtract(haystack, pattern[, index])
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Alias: <code>REGEXP_EXTRACT(haystack, pattern[, index])</code>.</p><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The string to search within. String.</li><li><code>pattern</code>: The regular expression pattern with capturing groups, using re2 regular expression syntax. String.</li><li><code>index</code>: An integer (0-based) specifying which capturing group to extract. 0 extracts the entire match. Defaults to 1. UInt or Int. Optional.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>The extracted substring corresponding to the specified capturing group. String.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    regexpExtract(&#x27;100-200&#x27;, &#x27;(\\d+)-(\\d+)&#x27;, 1),
    regexpExtract(&#x27;100-200&#x27;, &#x27;(\\d+)-(\\d+)&#x27;, 2),
    regexpExtract(&#x27;100-200&#x27;, &#x27;(\\d+)-(\\d+)&#x27;, 0),
    regexpExtract(&#x27;100-200&#x27;, &#x27;(\\d+)-(\\d+)&#x27;)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Result:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─regexpExtract(&#x27;100-200&#x27;, &#x27;(\\d+)-(\\d+)&#x27;, 1)─┬─regexpExtract(&#x27;100-200&#x27;, &#x27;(\\d+)-(\\d+)&#x27;, 2)─┬─regexpExtract(&#x27;100-200&#x27;, &#x27;(\\d+)-(\\d+)&#x27;, 0)─┬─regexpExtract(&#x27;100-200&#x27;, &#x27;(\\d+)-(\\d+)&#x27;)─┐

A subsequence can be derived by deleting zero or more characters from the original string without changing the order of the remaining characters.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">hasSubsequence(haystack, needle)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: The string to search within. String.</li><li><code>needle</code>: The subsequence to search for. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Returns 1 if <code>needle</code> is a subsequence of <code>haystack</code>, otherwise returns 0. UInt8.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT hasSubsequence(&#x27;garbage&#x27;, &#x27;arg&#x27;)

String.</li><li><code>needle</code>: The subsequence to search for. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Returns 1 if <code>needle</code> is a subsequence of <code>haystack</code> (case-insensitive), otherwise returns 0. </pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: String in which the search is performed. String or Enum.</li><li><code>token</code>: The token to search for. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Returns 1 if the <code>token</code> is found in the <code>haystack</code>, otherwise returns 0. UInt8.</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT hasToken(&#x27;Hello World&#x27;,&#x27;Hello&#x27;)

</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="hastokenornull" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">hasTokenOrNull<a class="headerlink" href="#hastokenornull" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Checks if a specific token is present in a string, returning 1 if found, 0 if not found, or <code>null</code> if the token is ill-formed.</p><h3 id="syntax" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Syntax<a class="headerlink" href="#syntax" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">hasTokenOrNull(haystack, token)
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="arguments" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Arguments<a class="headerlink" href="#arguments" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><code>haystack</code>: String in which the search is performed. String or Enum.</li><li><code>token</code>: The token to search for. String.</li></ul><h3 id="returns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Returns<a class="headerlink" href="#returns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Returns 1 if the <code>token</code> is present, 0 if not present, or <code>null</code> if the token is ill-formed. Nullable(UInt8).</p><h3 id="example" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Example<a class="headerlink" href="#example" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Where <code>hasToken</code> would throw an error for an ill-formed token, <code>hasTokenOrNull</code> returns <code>null</code> for an ill-formed token.</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT hasTokenOrNull(&#x27;Hello World&#x27;,&#x27;Hello,World&#x27;)
